            function holiday(p87, p88)
                local v96 = ({
                    ['01 01'] = '\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}',
                    [(function(p89)
                        local v90 = math.floor(p89 / 100)
                        local v91 = (15 - math.floor((13 + 8 * v90) / 25) + v90 - math.floor(v90 / 4)) % 30
                        local v92 = (4 + v90 - math.floor(v90 / 4)) % 7
                        local v93 = (19 * (p89 % 19) + v91) % 30
                        local v94 = (2 * (p89 % 4) + 4 * (p89 % 7) + 6 * v93 + v92) % 7
                        local v95 = 22 + v93 + v94

                        if v93 == 29 and v94 == 6 then
                            return '04 19'
                        elseif v93 == 28 and v94 == 6 then
                            return '04 18'
                        elseif v95 > 31 then
                            return ('04 %02d'):format(v95 - 31)
                        else
                            return ('03 %02d'):format(v95)
                        end
                    end)(tonumber(os.date('%Y')))] = '\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}',
                    ['10 31'] = '\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}',
                })[os.date('%m %d')]

                if v96 then
                    return ('%s %s %s'):format(v96, p87, v96)
                end

                local v97 = {
                    ['12 25'] = '\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}',
                }

                if p88 and p88.entireChristmas then
                    for v98 = 1, 31 do
                        v97['12 ' .. tostring(v98)] = ({
                            '\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}\u{fffd}',
                            '\u{fffd}\u{fffd}',
                        })[math.random(1, 2)]
                    end
                end
                if v97[os.date('%m %d')] then
                    local _ = ('%s %s %s').format
                end

                return p87
            end
            function formatDateTime(p99)
                local v109 = (function(p100)
                    local _dddTddd, v102 = p100:match('^(%d+-%d+-%d+)T(%d+:%d+:%d+)')

                    if not (_dddTddd and v102) then
                        return nil
                    end

                    local _ddd, v104, v105 = _dddTddd:match('(%d+)-(%d+)-(%d+)')
                    local _ddd2, v107, v108 = v102:match('(%d+):(%d+):(%d+)')

                    return os.time({
                        year = tonumber(_ddd),
                        month = tonumber(v104),
                        day = tonumber(v105),
                        hour = tonumber(_ddd2),
                        min = tonumber(v107),
                        sec = tonumber(v108),
                        isdst = false,
                    })
                end)(p99)

                if v109 then
                    local v110 = os.time()
                    local v111 = os.difftime(v110, v109)
                    local _ABdmY = os.date('%A %B %d/%m/%Y', v109)

                    if v111 < 86400 then
                        local v113 = math.floor(v111 / 3600)

                        return _ABdmY .. ' (' .. v113 .. ' hour' .. (v113 ~= 1 and 's' or '') .. ' ago)'
                    elseif v111 < 31536000 then
                        local v114 = math.floor(v111 / 86400)

                        return _ABdmY .. ' (' .. v114 .. ' day' .. (v114 ~= 1 and 's' or '') .. ' ago)'
                    else
                        local v115 = math.floor(v111 / 31536000)

                        return _ABdmY .. ' (' .. v115 .. ' year' .. (v115 ~= 1 and 's' or '') .. ' ago)'
                    end
                else
                    return 'Invalid date format'
                end
            end

            function WaitForChildWhichIsA(p146, p147, p148)
                local v149 = tick()

                if not p146:FindFirstChildWhichIsA(p147) then
                    repeat
                        task.wait()
                    until p146:FindFirstChildWhichIsA(p147) or p148 and tick() >= v149 + p148
                end

                return p146:FindFirstChildWhichIsA(p147) or nil
            end
            function getPlayer(p150, p151, p152)
                local v153 = _Players
                local v154, v155, v156 = pairs(v153:GetPlayers())

                while true do
                    local v157

                    v156, v157 = v154(v155, v156)

                    if v156 == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    if (v157.Name:lower():find('^' .. p150:lower()) or v157.DisplayName:lower():find('^' .. p150:lower())) and (v157 ~= _LocalPlayer or p152) then
                        return v157
                    end
                end

                if p151 and #_Players:GetChildren() >= 2 then
                    repeat
                        local v158 = _Players
                        local v159 = _Players:GetChildren()[math.random(1, #v158:GetChildren())]

                        task.wait()
                    until v159 ~= _LocalPlayer
                end

                return nil
            end
            function getAllPlayers()

                end

            end
            function getHighestStreak()
                local v165 = _Players
                local v166, v167, v168 = pairs(v165:GetPlayers())
                local v169 = 0
                local v170 = nil

                while true do
                    local v171

                    v168, v171 = v166(v167, v168)

                    if v168 == nil then
                        break
                    end

                    local v172 = getChar(v171)
                    local v173 = v172 and (v172:GetAttribute('CurrentStreak') or 0) or v172

                    if v172 then
                        if v169 < v173 then
                            v170 = v171
                            v169 = v173
                        end
                    end
                end

                return v170
            end
            function rejoin(p174)
                if typeof(p174) ~= 'table' or not p174 then
                    p174 = nil
                end

                _LocalPlayer:Kick(p174 and (p174.Message or 'Rejoining....') or 'Rejoining....')
                task.delay(p174 and p174.Delay or 0.1, function()
                    if u66 ~= 'VIPServer' then
                        _TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, game.JobId, _LocalPlayer)
                    else
                        _TeleportService:Teleport(game.PlaceId, _LocalPlayer)
                    end
                end)
            end

            local u175 = nil

            function patchCamera(p176)
                if p176:IsA('Camera') then
                    if u175 then
                        u175:Disconnect()

                        u175 = nil
                    end
                    if p176.CameraType ~= Enum.CameraType.Custom and Toggles.NoCameraAnimations.Value then
                        task.spawn(fixCam)
                    end

                    u175 = p176:GetPropertyChangedSignal('CameraType'):Connect(function()
                        if p176.CameraType ~= Enum.CameraType.Custom and Toggles.NoCameraAnimations.Value then
                            task.spawn(fixCam)
                        end
                    end)
                end
            end

            function getMagnitude(p180, p181)
                if typeof(p180) == 'number' then
                    p180 = Vector3.new(p180, p180, p180)
                end
                if typeof(p181) == 'number' then
                    p181 = Vector3.new(p181, p181, p181)
                end

                return (p180 - p181).Magnitude
            end
            function fixCam()
                if not getChar(_LocalPlayer) then
                    repeat
                        task.wait()
                    until getChar(_LocalPlayer)
                end

                local v182 = getChar(_LocalPlayer)
                local v183

                if v182 then
                    v183 = getHumanoid(v182)
                else
                    v183 = v182
                end
                if v182 and (v183 and workspace.CurrentCamera) then
                    local _CFrame = _Workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame

                    _Workspace.CurrentCamera:Destroy()

                    local _Camera = Instance.new('Camera', _Workspace)

                    _Camera.CameraType = 'Custom'
                    _Camera.CameraSubject = v183
                    _Camera.CFrame = _CFrame
                    _LocalPlayer.CameraMode = 'Classic'
                    v182:WaitForChild('Head', 1).Anchored = false
                end
            end
            function sendMsg(p186)
                if _TextChatService.ChatVersion ~= Enum.ChatVersion.LegacyChatService then
                    if _TextChatService.ChatVersion == Enum.ChatVersion.TextChatService then
                        local _TextChannels = _TextChatService.TextChannels
                        local _RBXGeneral = _TextChannels:FindFirstChild('RBXGeneral')

                        if _TextChannels and _RBXGeneral then
                            _RBXGeneral:SendAsync(p186)
                        end
                    end
                else
                    local _DefaultChatSystemChatEvents = _ReplicatedStorage:FindFirstChild('DefaultChatSystemChatEvents')
                    local v190

                    if _DefaultChatSystemChatEvents then
                        v190 = _DefaultChatSystemChatEvents:FindFirstChild('SayMessageRequest')
                    else
                        v190 = _DefaultChatSystemChatEvents
                    end
                    if _DefaultChatSystemChatEvents and v190 then
                        v190:FireServer(p186, 'all')
                    end
                end
            end
            function closestPlayer(p191, p192)
                local v193 = getChar

                if v193 then
                    v193 = getChar(_LocalPlayer)
                end

                local _huge = math.huge
                local v195 = _Players
                local v196, v197, v198 = pairs(v195:GetPlayers())
                local v199 = nil

                while true do
                    local v200

                    v198, v200 = v196(v197, v198)

                    if v198 == nil then
                        break
                    end
                    if getChar(v200) and v200 ~= _LocalPlayer then
                        local v201 = getChar(v200)
                        local v202 = getHumanoid(v201)

                        if v202 and v202.Health ~= 0 then
                            if v201 then
                                v201 = getRoot(v201)
                            end

                            local v203 = nil

                            if p191 then
                                v203 = (u6.Hit.p - v201.Position).Magnitude
                            elseif not p191 then
                                v203 = (getRoot(v193).Position - v201.Position).Magnitude
                            end
                            if v203 < _huge then
                                if p192 then
                                    if not isFlung(v200) then
                                        v199 = v200
                                        _huge = v203
                                    end
                                elseif not p192 then
                                    v199 = v200
                                    _huge = v203
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

                return v199
            end
            function closestPlayerV2(p204, p205)
                local v206 = getChar(_LocalPlayer)
                local v207

                    v207 = v206

                local v208 = nil

                            end

                            else
                                v217 = v215

                                local v218 = nil

                                    local v220 = _UserInputService

                                    v218 = (Vector2.new(v219.X, v219.Y) - v220:GetMouseLocation()).Magnitude
                                elseif not p204 then
                                    v218 = (v207.Position - v216.Position).Magnitude
                                end

                                        end
                                    elseif not p205 then
                                        _huge2 = v218
                                        v208 = v214
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

                return v208
            end
            function heartbeatTp(p221)
                local v222 = getChar(_LocalPlayer)
                local u223

                if v222 then
                    u223 = getRoot(v222)
                else
                    u223 = v222
                end
                if v222 and u223 then
                    task.spawn(function()
                        _RenderStepped:Once(function()
                            u223.Velocity = Vector3.new()

                            _Heartbeat:Wait()

                            u223.Velocity = Vector3.new()
                        end)
                    end)
                    _Heartbeat:Once(function()
                        u223.CFrame = p221
                    end)
                end
            end
            function breakVelocity(p224)
                assert(p224:IsA('BodyVelocity'), "Error Occured at function 'breakVelocity', Argument 1 must be a 'BodyVelocity'.")

                p224.MaxForce = Vector3.zero
                p224.Velocity = Vector3.zero

                _RenderStepped:Wait()
                p224:Destroy()
            end
            function clearVelocity()

                    v225 = getChar(_LocalPlayer)

                if v225 then

                    while true do

                        if v228 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if v229:IsA('BodyVelocity') and (v229 ~= BG and v229 ~= BV) then

                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            function randomAlphabeticalString(p230)
                local v231 = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ'
                local v232 = ''

                for _ = 1, p230 or math.random(3, 20)do
                    local v233 = math.random(1, #v231)

                    v232 = v232 .. v231:sub(v233, v233)
                end

                return v232
            end

                local v238 = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ '
                local v239 = ''

                for v240 = 1, utf8.len(v236)do
                    local v241 = string.sub(v236, utf8.offset(v236, v240), utf8.offset(v236, v240 + 1) - 1)
                    local v242 = string.find(v238, v241, 1, true)

                    if v242 then
                        v239 = v239 .. string.sub(p235, utf8.offset(p235, v242), utf8.offset(p235, v242 + 1) - 1) .. (v237 and '\20' or '')
                    else
                        v239 = v239 .. v241 .. (v237 and '\20' or '')
                    end

                return v239

            function createCaseInsensitivePattern(p243)
                local v244 = ''

                for v245 = 1, #p243 do
                    local v246 = p243:sub(v245, v245)

                    if v246:lower() ~= v246:upper() then
                        v244 = v244 .. '[' .. v246:upper() .. v246:lower() .. ']'
                    else
                        v244 = v244 .. v246
                    end
                end

                return v244
            end
            function convertToCyrillic(p247)
                local v248 = ''
                local v249 = {
                    A = '\u{fffd}',
                    a = '\u{fffd}',
                    O = '\u{fffd}',
                    o = '\u{fffd}',
                    E = '\u{fffd}',
                    e = '\u{fffd}',
                }

                for v250 = 1, #p247 do
                    local v251 = p247:sub(v250, v250)

                    v248 = v248 .. (v249[v251] or v251)
                end

                return v248
            end
            function flingTp(p252)
                local v253 = getChar

                if v253 then
                    v253 = getChar(p252)
                end

                local v254 = getRoot(v253)
                local v255 = getHumanoid(v253)

                if v253 and (v254 and v255) then
                    local v256 = math.random(1, 2)

                    if v256 == 1 then
                        return v254.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-180, 180)), math.rad(0), math.rad(math.random(-180, 180)))
                    end
                    if v256 == 2 then
                        return CFrame.new(v254.Position) * (CFrame.new(math.random(-5, 5), math.random(-2.5, 2.5), math.random(-5, 5)) + v255.MoveDirection * v254.Velocity.Magnitude / 1.25) * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(math.random(-180, 180)), math.rad(0), math.rad(math.random(-180, 180)))
                    end
                end
            end
            function isFlung(p257)

            function isDeathBlowing(p260)
                local v261 = getChar(p260)
                local v262

                    v262 = getRoot(v261)
                else
                    v262 = v261
                end

                local v263

                if v261 then
                    v263 = getHumanoid(v261)
                else
                    v263 = v261

                if v261 and (v262 and v263) then

                    while true do
                        local v267

                        if v266 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if v267:IsA('Tool') and v267.Name == 'Death Blow' then
                            return true
                        end
                    end

                    if isAnimPlaying(v263, '15128849047') then
                        return true
                    end

                    local v268 = _Players
                    local v269, v270, v271 = pairs(v268:GetPlayers())

                    while true do
                        local v272

                        v271, v272 = v269(v270, v271)

                        if v271 == nil then

                            local v273 = getChar(v272)

                            if v273 then
                                v274 = getRoot(v273)
                            else
                                v274 = v273

                            if v273 then
                                v275 = getHumanoid(v273)
                            else
                                v275 = v273
                            end
                            if v273 and (v274 and (v275 and (v274.Position - v262.Position).Magnitude <= 100)) then
                                local v276, v277, v278 = pairs(v273:GetChildren())

                                while true do
                                    local v279

                                    v278, v279 = v276(v277, v278)

                                    if v278 == nil then
                                        break
                                    end
                                    if v279:IsA('Tool') and v279.Name == 'Death Blow' then
                                        return
                                    end
                                end

                                if isAnimPlaying(v275, '15128849047') then
                                    return true
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    end
                end

                return false
            end

            function loadAnim(p331, p332, p333)
                if not (p331 and p332) then
                    return nil
                end

                local v334 = 'rbxassetid://' .. tostring(p332):match('%d+')
                local _Animation = Instance.new('Animation')
                local v336 = nil

                if p333 then
                    if p333 == 'Server' then
                        _Animation.AnimationId = 'rbxassetid://0'
                        v336 = p331:LoadAnimation(_Animation)
                        _Animation.AnimationId = v334
                    elseif p333 == 'Client' then
                        _Animation.AnimationId = v334
                        v336 = p331:LoadAnimation(_Animation)
                        _Animation.AnimationId = 'rbxassetid://0'
                    end
                else
                    _Animation.AnimationId = v334
                    v336 = p331:LoadAnimation(_Animation)
                end

                return v336
            end
            function loadSound(p337, p338)
                if not (p337 and p338) then
                    return nil
                end

                local v339 = 'rbxassetid://' .. tostring(p338):match('%d+')
                local _Sound = Instance.new('Sound')

                _Sound.Parent = p337
                _Sound.SoundId = v339

                return _Sound
            end
            function stopAllAnims(p341, p342)
                local v343 = not p341 and getChar(_LocalPlayer)

                if v343 then
                    v343 = getHumanoid(getChar(_LocalPlayer))
                end
                if v343 then
                    if not (v343:IsA('Humanoid') or v343:IsA('Animator')) then
                        return warn("Error occured at function 'stopAllAnims', Argument 1 must be a valid animator.")
                    end
                    if p342 then
                        local v344, v345, v346 = pairs(v343:GetPlayingAnimationTracks())

                        while true do
                            local v347

                            v346, v347 = v344(v345, v346)

                            if v346 == nil then
                                break
                            end
                            if typeof(p342) ~= 'table' then
                                if v347.Animation.AnimationId:match(tostring(p342):match('%d+')) then
                                    v347:Stop()
                                end
                            else
                                local v348, v349, v350 = pairs(p342)

                                while true do
                                    local v351

                                    v350, v351 = v348(v349, v350)

                                    if v350 == nil then
                                        break
                                    end
                                    if v347.Animation.AnimationId:match(tostring(v351):match('%d+')) then
                                        v347:Stop()
                                    end
                                end
                            end
                        end
                    else
                        local v352, v353, v354 = pairs(v343:GetPlayingAnimationTracks())

                        while true do
                            local v355

                            v354, v355 = v352(v353, v354)

                            if v354 == nil then
                                break
                            end

                            v355:Stop()
                        end
                    end
                end
            end
            function deleteAllInstances(p356, p357)
                local v358 = p356 or getChar(_LocalPlayer)

                if v358 and p357 then
                    local v359, v360, v361 = pairs(v358:GetChildren())

                    while true do
                        local v362

                        v361, v362 = v359(v360, v361)

                        if v361 == nil then
                            break
                        end
                        if typeof(p357) ~= 'table' then
                            if v362.Name:lower() == p357:lower() then
                                v362:Destroy()
                            end
                        else
                            local v363, v364, v365 = pairs(p357)

                    'beamed',

                                v743.CanQuery = false

                                                Dash = Enum.KeyCode.S,

                                                getgenv().desync = nil
                                            end
                                        end)
                                    end
                                else
                                    task.spawn(pcall, deleteNew, p1001, false)
                                end
                            end

                            return
                        end
                    end)
                end

                    '50%',
                    '75%',
                    '100%',
                    '125%',
                    '150%',
                    '175%',
                    '200%',
                },
                Default = '100%',
                Text = 'DPI Scale',
                Callback = function(p1676)
                    local v1677 = p1676:gsub('%%', '')

                    u477:SetDPIScale((tonumber(v1677)))
                end,
            })
            _Menu:AddDivider()
            _Menu:AddLabel('Menu Bind'):AddKeyPicker('MenuKeybind', {
                Default = 'RightControl',
                NoUI = true,
                Text = 'Menu keybind',
            })
            _Menu:AddButton('Unload', function()
                u477:Unload()
            end)
            _Menu:AddButton('Rejoin', rejoin)

            u43[#u43 + 1] = _RenderStepped:Connect(function()
                if not Toggles.ShowUntoggledKeybinds.Value then
                    local _KeybindsToggle = Options.FlyBind.KeybindsToggle

                    if Toggles.Fly.Value then
                        _KeybindsToggle:SetVisibility(true)
                    else
                        _KeybindsToggle:SetVisibility(false)
                    end

                    local _KeybindsToggle2 = Options.AnimeTPKeybind.KeybindsToggle

                    if Toggles.AnimeTeleportation.Value then
                        _KeybindsToggle2:SetVisibility(true)
                    else
                        _KeybindsToggle2:SetVisibility(false)
                    end

                    local _KeybindsToggle3 = Options['L-OnKeybind'].KeybindsToggle

                    if Toggles['Lock-on'].Value then
                        _KeybindsToggle3:SetVisibility(true)
                    else
                        _KeybindsToggle3:SetVisibility(false)
                    end

                    local _KeybindsToggle4 = Options.OrbitBind.KeybindsToggle

                    if Toggles.Orbit.Value then
                        _KeybindsToggle4:SetVisibility(true)
                    else
                        _KeybindsToggle4:SetVisibility(false)
                    end

                    local _KeybindsToggle5 = Options.TP1Bind.KeybindsToggle

                    if Toggles.TP1.Value then
                        _KeybindsToggle5:SetVisibility(true)
                    else
                        _KeybindsToggle5:SetVisibility(false)
                    end

                    local _KeybindsToggle6 = Options.TP2Bind.KeybindsToggle

                    if Toggles.TP2.Value then
                        _KeybindsToggle6:SetVisibility(true)
                    else
                        _KeybindsToggle6:SetVisibility(false)
                    end

                    local _KeybindsToggle7 = Options.VelocitySpoofBind.KeybindsToggle

                    if Toggles.VelocitySpoof.Value then
                        _KeybindsToggle7:SetVisibility(true)
                    else
                        _KeybindsToggle7:SetVisibility(false)
                    end
                end
            end)
            u477.ToggleKeybind = Options.MenuKeybind

            v478:SetLibrary(u477)
            v479:SetLibrary(u477)
            v479:IgnoreThemeSettings()
            v479:SetIgnoreIndexes({
                'MenuKeybind',
            })
            v478:SetFolder('Phantasm')
            v479:SetFolder('Phantasm/The Strongest Battlegrounds')
            v479:BuildConfigSection(v484['UI Settings'])
            v478:ApplyToTab(v484['UI Settings'])
            v479:LoadAutoloadConfig()
            task.spawn(function()
                if u10 then
                    u10.Text = string.format('Loaded in %.1f seconds!', tick() - u1)

                    task.wait(2)

                    while true do
                        if u10 then
                            u10.Text = u10.Text:sub(1, -2)
                        end

                        task.wait(0.03)

                        if u10 and u10.Text == '' or not u10 then
                            u10.Parent:Destroy()
                        end
                    end
                else
                    return
                end
            end)
            u477:Notify({
                Title = bypassText('Phantasm'),
                Description = bypassText('Script loaded successfully!'),
                Time = 3,
                SoundId = u41.Notification,
            })
        end
    else
        return
    end
end
